<h2 id="patch-top"></h2>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
		‘Tis (the end) of the season so we're here to wrap things up with 13.24!<br/>
<br/>
		It's the last patch of the year and the next time you'll hear from us will be in patch 14.1 alongside all of the exciting gameplay changes. But that doesn't mean we don't have any presents for you this patch…<br/>
<br/>
		Our first gift is the newest addition to our roster—Hwei, the Visionary. With a whole palette of abilities at his disposal, Hwei provides players the opportunity to flex their big brains by choosing the perfect ability for each situation. So if you're interested in complex champions then this one's for you!<br/>
<br/>
		We also have the widely-requested return of Arena this patch! With over 180 balance adjustments, Arena is coming back better than ever. We're also adding in the ability to queue with up to 4 players or queue with a full party of 8 so you and your friends can really find out who the best gladiator is. With new mechanics, Augments, and cameos, there's plenty to learn and experiment with. So be sure to check it out.<br/>
<br/>
		In other news, we also have the last Clash of the year coming for ARAM, a delightful batch of new Winterblessed skins, a new Mythic Shop rotation, and more. So check out the full patch notes below and see you in 2024!<br/>
<br/>
		Jazzed about the new TFT set? Well make sure you stay up to date and avoid any unwelcome mix ups by checking out the <em>TFT patch notes <a href="https://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/news/game-updates/teamfight-tactics-patch-13-24-notes/">here</a>!</em>
</blockquote>

<h4 class="change-title" id="patch-december-14-2023-arena-update">December 14, 2023 Arena Update</h4>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Arena Augment Changes</h4><br/>
<p class="summary">Due to balance issues, the following augments have been removed from Arena:</p>
<ul>
<li>Desecrator</li>
<li>Doomsayer</li>
<li>Deathtouch</li>
<li>Plaguebearer</li>
<li>Dark Blessing</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="white-stone accent-before">

<h4 class="change-title" id="patch-december-12-2023-balance-adjustments-and-arena">December 12, 2023 Balance Adjustments &amp; Arena</h4>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Balance Adjustments (Summoner’s Rift)</h4><br/>
<strong>Corki</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base AD</strong>: 55 ⇒ 59</li>
<li><strong>AD Growth</strong>: 2.8 ⇒ 2.5</li>
<li><strong>Base Health</strong>: 588 ⇒ 610</li>
<li><strong>Health Growth</strong>: 105 ⇒ 103</li>
</ul><strong>Hwei</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base Health</strong>: 550 ⇒ 580</li>
<li><strong>Base Movement Speed</strong>: 325 ⇒ 330</li>
<li><strong>Base Mana</strong>: 445 ⇒ 480</li>
<li><strong>WW Shield Timing</strong>: As soon as the cast finishes ⇒ Instantly</li>
<li><strong>WW Base Shield Values</strong>: 90/110/130/150/170 ⇒ 100/125/150/175/200</li>
<li><strong>EW Setup Delay</strong>: 0.7 seconds ⇒ 0.65 seconds</li>
<li><strong>EW Fire Delay</strong>: 0.35 seconds ⇒ 0.3 seconds</li>
<li><strong>EW Chase Range</strong>: 500 ⇒ 600</li>
<li><strong>EW Linger Duration</strong>: 1.35-3 seconds based on travel distance ⇒ 3 seconds</li>
</ul><strong>Naafiri</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>E Cooldown</strong>: 11/10.5/10/9.5/9 seconds ⇒ 10/9.5/9/8.5/8 seconds</li>
</ul><strong>Neeko</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>Bugfix</strong>: Fixed a bug that caused Neeko to be able to adjust certain unintentional stats using her passive transformation.</li>
</ul>
<strong>Orianna</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base Health</strong>: 600 ⇒ 585</li>
<li><strong>W Movement Speed Modifier</strong>: 30-50% (based on rank) ⇒ 20-40% (based on rank) </li>
</ul>
<strong>Sylas</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>W Magic Damage</strong>: 70/105/140/175/210 (+90% AP) ⇒ 65/100/135/170/205 (+80% AP)</li>
<li><strong>W Heal</strong>: 20/40/60/80/100 (+40% AP) ⇒ 20/40/60/80/100 (+35% AP) <em>(Note: heal is still doubled at ~60% missing health)</em></li>
</ul><strong>Syndra</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>Q Magic Damage</strong>: 75/110/145/180/215 (+70% AP) ⇒ 75/110/145/180/215 (+60% AP)</li>
<li><strong>Bugfix</strong>: Fixed a bug that caused Syndra to lose her passive 15% bonus AP buff when revived by a Zilean ultimate or Guardian Angel.</li>
</ul><strong>Warwick</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>Q Monster Percent Health Cap</strong>: 100/125/150/175/200 ⇒ 150/165/180/195/210</li>
<li><strong>W Active Cooldown</strong>: 120/105/90/75/60 seconds ⇒ 100/85/70/55/40 seconds</li>
<li><strong>W Bonus Movement Speed</strong>: 35/40/45/50/55% ⇒ 35/42.5/50/57.5/65%</li>
</ul><strong>Yone</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>W Base Shield</strong>: 60-80 (based on level) ⇒ 40-90 (based on level)</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Arena Balance Adjustments</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Hexgate Cooldown</strong>: 8 seconds ⇒ 12 seconds</li>
<li><strong>Grievous Wounds from Ring of Fire (per second)</strong>: 15% ⇒ 20%</li>
<li><span class="new">new</span><strong>Good Luck Shielding This</strong>: Ring of Fire now reduces shielding in addition to healing.</li>
<li><strong>Plaguebearer Tick Rate</strong>: every 1 second ⇒ every 1.5 seconds</li>
<li><strong>Bugfix</strong>: Fixed a bug that caused Bread and Butter/Jam/Cheese to not grant Ability Haste to abilities whose cooldown scales with Attack Speed.</li>
</ul>
</div>

<li><strong>Jhin</strong>: Percent Movement Speed on Critical Strikes: 80% <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 60%. Q Damage: 70-310 (+80-120% AD) <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 65-245 (+70-110% AD)</li>
<li><strong>Karthus</strong>: Added Bonus Maximum Health: 0-200 (levels 1-18). R Damage: 200/350/500 (+75% AP) <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 350/550/750 (+100% AP)</li>
<li><strong>Leona</strong>: Q Cooldown: 5 seconds <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 6 seconds. W Cooldown: 14-10 seconds <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 14-12 seconds</li>
<li><strong>Neeko</strong>: Added Bonus Maximum Health: 0-200 (levels 1-18). Q Base Damage: 80/125/170/215/260 <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 90/140/190/240/290</li>

<li><strong>Orbital Laser</strong>: Magic Damage per Tick: 30-90 <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 40-120</li>

<h4 class="change-title" id="patch-december-7-2023-blue-essence-emporium-and-hwei-adjustments">December 7, 2023 Blue Essence Emporium and Hwei Adjustments</h4>

<div>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
						Blue Essence Emporium is back! You’ll be able to spend your Blue Essence on chromas released prior to July 2023, accessories, and more starting on December 13, 21:00 UTC. We’ve also brought back the highly requested mystery wards and icons so definitely take advantage of that while you can. The Emporium will remain open until December 27, 21:00 UTC, so make sure to drop by and drop that Blue Essence!
					</blockquote>
</div>
<ul>
<li>Due to technical issues we’ve disabled the ability to gift mystery wards and icons, however this feature will return in a future Blue Essence Emporium.</li>
</ul>

<li><strong>EQ - Grim Visage Damage</strong>: 60/90/120/150/180 (+55% AP) ⇒ 60/90/120/150/180 <strong>(+60% AP)</strong></li>

<header class="header-primary">
<h2 id="patch-cast-at-maximum-range-toggle">Cast at Maximum Range Toggle</h2>
</header>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					In this patch we've added a new toggle setting that will affect how champions cast their abilities when the player inputs the command outside of max range. Go to Options &gt; Game &gt; Clamp Cast Target Location within Max Range and BOOM. With the toggle turned on abilities will automatically be cast at max range if the ability was cast outside of the ability's casting range
				</blockquote>
</div>

<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-hwei"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/hwei/">Hwei</a></h3>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Every mark should have meaning. Make your mark with Hwei on December 6, 2023 at 21:00 UTC.
				</blockquote>

<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/azir/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Azir.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-azir"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/azir/">Azir</a></h3>
<p class="summary">W damage increased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					We're happy that Azir has a new suite of items to consider and that Nashor's Tooth finally functions as many players expect it should. Looking into his builds, Liandry's-Nashor's, Luden's-Nashor's, and Crown-Nashor's are all performing a little bit worse than they were in the last patch so we'll be walking back one of the smaller nerfs he received in 13.23.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/AzirW.png"/>W - Arise!</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 2-77 (levels 10-18) (+50/65/80/95/110) (+55% AP) ⇒ 2-77 (levels 10-18) <strong>(+50/67/84/101/118)</strong> (+55% AP)</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/braum/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Braum.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-braum"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/braum/">Braum</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Base mana regeneration increased. R knock up duration increased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Braum has some very sharp matchups in his current state. He's extremely strong as counter-engage into vanguards and is very weak in most ranged matchups where he doesn't really get to do anything. While he should be best served as a true defensive warden, we'd like to give him more agency in those weaker matchups. Mana regen should allow him more freedom to use abilities while a better Glacial Fissure will let him accomplish more outside of lane, while still being suboptimal for pure engage.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Base Stats</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base Mana Regeneration</strong>: 6 ⇒ 7</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/BraumRWrapper.png"/>R - Glacial Fissure</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Minimum Knock Up Duration</strong>: 0.3 seconds ⇒ 0.6 seconds</li>
<li><strong>Secondary Target Knock Up Duration</strong>: 0.3 seconds ⇒ 0.6 seconds</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/briar/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Briar.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-briar"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/briar/">Briar</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Base armor decreased, attack speed ratio increased. Q damage increased. W bonus attack speed decreased. E damage resistance decreased, healing decreased. R damage decreased, damage type changed to magic.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Briar continues to devour her opposition in the jungle as players continue to get better at her, so we need to pull her power back a bit more. While we're nerfing all her builds with these changes, we're targeting lethality builds more. To that end, we're shifting R to magic damage and throwing in a buff to her attack speed ratio. With the attack speed ratio change, Briar's overall attack speed will be higher when building Stridebreaker, while staying close to the same on builds that don't purchase any attack speed. This should help make up for the nerf to W.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Base Stats</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base Armor</strong>: 32 ⇒ 30</li>
<li><strong>Attack Speed Ratio</strong>: 0.644 ⇒ 0.669 <em>(Note: Attack speed at level 1 is unchanged.)</em></li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/BriarQ.png"/>Q - Head Rush</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 60/95/130/165/200 (+80% bonus AD) ⇒ <strong>60/90/120/150/180</strong> (+80% bonus AD)</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/BriarW.png"/>W - Blood Frenzy</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Bonus Attack Speed</strong>: 60/75/90/105/120% ⇒ 55/70/85/100/115%</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/BriarE.png"/>E - Chilling Scream</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage Reduction</strong>: 40% ⇒ 35%</li>
<li><strong>Healing</strong>: 10/11.5/13/14.5/16% of Maximum Health ⇒ 9/10/11/12/13% of Maximum Health</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/BriarR.png"/>R - Certain Death</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 150/300/450 (+75% bonus AD) (+110% AP) Physical Damage ⇒ 150/300/450 <strong>(+50% bonus AD) (+120% AP) Magic Damage</strong></li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/galio/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Galio.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-galio"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/galio/">Galio</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Q cooldown decreased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					We're back again to follow up on our Galio changes as he's still not performing as well as we'd like him to. Our last two adjustments were intended to buff Galio's unique strengths such as his semi-global ultimate and anti-mage durability. This round, we're giving Galio players more individual power in the form of lowering his Q cooldown so he can better duel with his opponents because it's currently quite high despite being his primary poke/clear ability.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/GalioQ.png"/>Q - Winds of War</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Cooldown</strong>: 12/11.5/11/10.5/10 seconds ⇒ 12/11/10/9/8 seconds</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/gragas/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Gragas.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-gragas"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/gragas/">Gragas</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Passive cooldown now decreases with level.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Back in patch 13.12 we released a Gragas nerf that increased his passive cooldown from 8 to 12 seconds. We've updated this to have his passive scale down as the game goes on. This is intended to give Gragas players more frequent access to his passive at later points in the game so he can sustain better during teamfights and while side-laning, but without reintroducing the oppressive sustain he had earlier this year.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/passive/GragasPassiveHeal.png"/>Passive - Happy Hour</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Cooldown</strong>: 12 seconds ⇒ 12/10/8/6 seconds (levels 1/6/11/16)</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/ivern/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Ivern.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-ivern"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/ivern/">Ivern</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Base health decreased. E slow decreased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Ivern remained unaffected when other junglers' clears were made slightly slower in patch 13.20. As a result, he's become one of the best junglers in the current game. We'd just like to take a small swing at his high base health in hopes of balancing him against other junglers and making him a bit more vulnerable to invades. Because Friend of the Forest's health cost is based on Ivern's base health, this change will have no impact on his ability to clear camps unless he gets directly damaged by his enemies. Beyond that, we're taking a small bite out of Triggerseed's slow as it locks down opponents a bit harder than we'd like, considering he has other harder-to-land crowd control abilities.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Base Stats</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base Health</strong>: 655 ⇒ 630</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/IvernE.png"/>E - Triggerseed</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Slow</strong>: 50/55/60/65/70% ⇒ 45/50/55/60/65%</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/ksante/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/KSante.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-ksante"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/k-sante/">K'Sante</a></h3>
<p class="summary">W mana cost decreased, damage increased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					We overshot our nerf on K'Sante last patch but we're happy with the parts of his kit that we addressed. Now that we've nerfed the lane safety provided by his Q, we're aiming to buff him by making Path Maker a more active part of his laning phase through softening its mana cost and then increasing his reliance on gold income via these ratio buffs.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/KSanteW.png"/>W - Path Maker</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Mana Cost</strong>: 60/65/70/75/80 ⇒ 40/45/50/55/60</li>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 20/40/60/80/100 (+50% AD) (+30% bonus armor) (+30% bonus magic resistance) (+6/7/8/9/10% target's maximum health) ⇒ 20/40/60/80/100 (+50% AD) <strong>(+50% bonus armor) (+50% bonus magic resistance)</strong> (+6/7/8/9/10% target's maximum health)</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/leona/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Leona.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-leona"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/leona/">Leona</a></h3>
<p class="summary">W bonus armor and MR increased. R damage increased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Leona isn't the shining beam of light she once was and could use a bit more power. In order to get her glimmering again we're aiming to enhance her ability to all-in, as she has to commit harder to her engages than other similar supports and her engage capability is a primary reason for picking her. We're targeting her R damage and late-game W resistances specifically to give her more power in a way that doesn't affect her first few levels.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/LeonaSolarBarrier.png"/>W - Eclipse</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Bonus Armor</strong>: 20/25/30/35/40 (+20% bonus armor) ⇒ <strong>20/27.5/35/42.5/50</strong> (+20% bonus armor)</li>
<li><strong>Bonus Magic Resistance</strong>: 20/25/30/35/40 (+20% bonus magic resistance) ⇒ <strong>20/27.5/35/42.5/50</strong> (+20% bonus magic resistance)</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/LeonaSolarFlare.png"/>R - Solar Flare</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 100/175/250 (+80% AP) ⇒ <strong>150/225/300</strong> (+80% AP)</li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/lucian/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Lucian.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-lucian"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/lucian/">Lucian</a></h3>
<p class="summary">E cooldown decreased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Lucian is currently struggling in solo queue and could use a helping hand. Since our last two adjustments were to his Vigilance passive (which he's reliant on his team for) we're now choosing a buff that will give Lucian players themselves more power. We've decided to reduce his E cooldown, as Lucian is supposed to be powerful early, and this cooldown has some room to go down and still scale to the same level by mid game.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/LucianE.png"/>E - Relentless Pursuit</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Cooldown</strong>: 22/20/18/16/14 seconds ⇒ 19/17.75/16.5/15.25/14 seconds</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/mordekaiser/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Mordekaiser.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-mordekaiser"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/mordekaiser/">Mordekaiser</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Q damage increased. R now reveals the target upon initial cast.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Mordekaiser isn't performing particularly well at the moment, so we're taking a look under his rusty metal hood. First, a quality of life change to prevent the fog of war from canceling his ultimate. Second, he's gettingan AP ratio buff to his Q with the goal of letting him build ability power in more of his games, instead of transitioning into tank items quite so quickly.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/MordekaiserQ.png"/>Q - Obliterate</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 75/95/115/135/155 (+5-139 (based on level)) (+60% AP) ⇒ 75/95/115/135/155 (+5-139 (based on level)) <strong>(+70% AP)</strong></li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/MordekaiserR.png"/>R - Realm of Death</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>You Can Run…</strong>: Casting Realm of Death will now reveal the target upon starting the cast. This means that walking into a brush while Mordekaiser is casting his R will no longer cancel the spell. Note: The target will not be revealed for the entire duration of the spell, so you can still hide on bush if one comes with you to the Realm.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/qiyana/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Qiyana.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-qiyana"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/qiyana/">Qiyana</a></h3>
<p class="summary">Base mana and mana growth increased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Qiyana is a very high-skill-cap champion who only performs above average in very high-skill brackets. We don't expect to truly change that fact, but we'd still like to make her a little more forgiving to play. We noticed that she's a pretty frequent Manamune purchaser, so with these changes we'd like for you to have your cake and eat it too. If you don't buy Manamune, you have more mana to play with, and thus, don't need Tear as badly. However, if you do buy Manamune, having more total mana means more bonus AD and ability damage. So everyone wins! Except maybe her opponents. They might lose.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Base Stats</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base Mana</strong>: 325 ⇒ 375</li>
<li><strong>Mana Growth</strong>: 50 ⇒ 60</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">

<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-velkoz"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/vel-koz/">Vel'Koz</a></h3>
<p class="summary">W and E Bugfixes</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					As part of this patch we had planned to do some follow up work to Vel'Koz but the changes weren't quite ready to ship. Part of those changes were bug fixes which were ready, so instead of waiting to patch in both at the same time we'll be patching the bug fixes a bit earlier.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/VelkozW.png"/>W - Void Rift</h4>
<ul>
<li>Fixed a bug where the first half of the rift would fizzle if Vel'Koz died directly after casting.</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/VelkozE.png"/>E - Tectonic Disruption</h4>
<ul>
<li>Fixed a bug where the spell would fizzle out when V'K flashes or is knocked back at max range.</li>
<li>Tectonic Disruption's missile will now spawn at Vel'koz's original location if he flashes or is knocked back during the cast.</li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<a class="reference-link" href="http://leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/zeri/"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/champion/Zeri.png"/></a>
<h3 class="change-title" id="patch-zeri"><a href="http://www.leagueoflegends.com/en-us/champions/zeri/">Zeri</a></h3>
<p class="summary">AD growth increased. W damage increased.</p>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Zeri hasn't been zipping and zapping around like she used to and her battery power level is low, so we're giving her a small damage buff with the goal to amp her up ever so slightly.
				</blockquote>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Base Stats</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>AD Growth</strong>: 1.3 ⇒ 2</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title ability-title"><img src="https://am-a.akamaihd.net/image?f=http://ddragon.leagueoflegends.com/cdn/13.23.1/img/spell/ZeriW.png"/>W - Ultrashock Laser</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Damage</strong>: 20/60/100/140/180 (+130% AD) (+25% AP) ⇒ <strong>30/70/110/150/190</strong> (+130% AD) (+25% AP)</li>
</ul>
</div>

<header class="header-primary">
<h2 id="patch-ranked-season-schedule-update">Ranked Season Schedule Update</h2>
</header>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="patch-change-block white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<p>Season 2023 Split 2 ends at 23:59:59 January 9, 2024 according to your regional local time.</p>
<p>Season 2024 Split 1 starts at 12:00:00 January 10, 2024 according to regional local time everywhere except for LA1 and NA1:</p>
<ul>
<li>LA1 starts at 9am, Jan 10 CST</li>
<li>NA1 starts at 7am, Jan 10 PST</li>
</ul>
<p>The season transition experience will be similar to what we had in the past: Ranked queues will be disabled for a couple of hours, and will be brought back as soon as 14.1 is up, and a couple of hours after that, Split 1 will be officially launched! The ranked games played during the downtime won't count towards your new season progression.</p>
<p>Shard transfers will be disabled before season end, and re-enabled after all end of season rewards are granted.</p><br/>
<br/>

<header class="header-primary">
<h2 id="patch-arena-returns">Arena Returns</h2>
</header>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
					Hey Gladiators! We're incredibly excited for you to see all the new items, augments, and balance updates we've been working on. There are a lot of changes to cover! You can find the nitty gritty details below, but if you want to get straight to the action, here is a quick summary of all the biggest things to look out for in the Rings of Wrath!
				</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>A huge amount of class and individual champion balance changes.</li>
<li>Hexgates have been added to all four Arenas!</li>
<li>Death is not the end! After a delay, you can revive your dead teammate by standing on their body!</li>
<li>We've removed the Naafiri, Samira, Shaco, Viego, Lux, Evelynn, and Jhin cameos, and we've added Sylas and Thresh cameos!</li>
<li>4 new items!</li>
<li>60 new Augments!</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<br/>
<div>
<blockquote class="blockquote context">
						Due to the large amount of balance adjustments being made this patch change lists will only contain the numbers being changed and not the entire equation as per usual.
					</blockquote>
</div>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Gameplay Updates</h4><br/>
<strong>Hexgates</strong>
<ul>
<li>Hexgates have been added to each of the 4 Rings of Wrath. They work just like they do on Hextech Rift and Howling Abyss and have a 7 second cooldown.</li>
</ul><br/>
<strong>Downed State/Reviving</strong>
<ul>
<li>When a champion dies for the first time each round, they become downed for 11-8 seconds (based on round number), after which they become revivable. If an ally stands near a revivable ally for 3 seconds, they are resurrected and healed by their ally for 150+75 per level.</li>
<li>Revive duration is cumulative. If you spend 1 second near your Downed ally, then leave and come back, they will only take 2 seconds to Revive.</li>
<li>Revive duration is decreased based on the reviver’s Heal/Shield Power, and also decreased based on how much less team health the reviver has than the enemy team.</li>
<li>When you are revived, you become Invulnerable, Untargetable, and unable to attack/cast for 0.75 seconds. You will also gain 30% damage reduction, 75% Move Speed, and 50% Tenacity decaying over 3 seconds (or 2.25 seconds after the invulnerability ends).</li>
<li>In order to revive an ally, the ally must not be reviving with another effect or ability such as Zilean’s R, Zac’s Passive, or Guardian Angel.</li>
</ul><br/>
<strong>Cameos</strong>
<ul>
<li>The following Cameos have been removed: Naafiri. Samira, Shaco, Viego, Lux, Evelynn, and Jhin</li>
<li>The following Cameos have been added: Sylas (At the start of the round, Sylas replaces Summoner Flee with a one-use random Ultimate) and Thresh (Thresh will occasionally throw out a Lantern. The Lantern continuously Shields and can be selected to be pulled to Thresh).</li>
</ul><br/>
<strong>New Items</strong>
<ul>
<li>Sword of the Blossoming Dawn: 40 Ability Power, 200 Health, 15% Heal and Shield Power, 15 Ability Haste. Passive Effervescence: Gain 1.2% Attack Speed for every 1% Heal and Shield Power you have. Passive Peppermint: On-Hit, heal the lowest health ally champion near you for 15-45 (+10% bonus AD) (+7% AP)</li>
<li>Perplexity: 70 Ability Power, 8% Move Speed, 22% Armor Penetration, 30% Magic Penetration. Passive Giant Slayer: Deal up to 22% bonus damage against champions with greater maximum Health than you.</li>
<li>Hellfire Hatchet: 40 Attack Damage, 12 Lethality, 15% Omnivamp. Passive Char: On-Hit or damaging an enemy with an active ability, heal for 2% of the Target's Current Health and apply 1 stack of Burn that deals 12% bonus AD (+10% AP) (+2% Missing Health) physical damage per second for 4 seconds.</li>
<li>Wordless Promise: 60 Ability Power, 15% Heal and Shield Power, 25 Ability Haste. Active - Promise: Make a Promise to an ally (90 second Cooldown). Passive Promise: Gain 20% of your Promised ally's Ability Power, and grant your Promised ally 20% of your Ability Haste.</li>
</ul><br/>
<strong>Augment Updates</strong>
<ul>
<li>Once two champions possess the same Augment, that Augment is removed from the pool.</li>
<li>60 Augments have been added to the Augment Pool! While we could share them all here, it’s more fun to enjoy exploring and experiencing them live. GLHF!</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Queue Changes</h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Maximum Party Size</strong>: 2 players ⇒ 4 players <em>(Note: when queuing with 3 players the party will be given the option to select who will be matched with a random player.)</em></li>
<li><strong>Rating Restrictions</strong>: Players with a Gladiator rating can only queue with other Gladiator rated players ⇒ Players with an 8,100 rating or higher can only queue with 1 other player, and players must be within 1,000 rating of one another to queue together</li>
<li><strong>Private Matchmaking</strong>: A full party of 8 players can queue together for an unrated game. There are no rating restrictions in private matches.</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Rating System Changes</h4>
<ul>
<li>Arena ratings from the initial launch have been reset, and all players will begin in Wood Tier with a 500 rating.</li>
<li><strong>Gold Tier Rating</strong>: 3200 ⇒ 3300</li>
<li><strong>Gladiator Tier Rating</strong>: 3800 ⇒ 4000</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">General Balance Adjustments</h4>
<ul>
<li>Health Bonus for Melee Champions: 200-700 (based on level)</li>
<li style="list-style: none"><span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> <span class="attribute-after">50-900 (based on level)</span></li>
<li>Health Bonus for Ranged Champions: 300-800 (based on level) <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 150-1150 (based on level)</li>
<li>Resist Bonus for Melee Champions: 4-8 (based on level) <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 8-36 (based on level)</li>
<li>Armor/MR Bonus for Ranged Champions: 2-4 (based on level <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 2-16 (based on level)</li>
<li>Attack Speed Bonus for Ranged Champions: 20% at all levels <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> Removed</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>

<li>Conquerer Post-Mitigation Healing: 8%/5% (melee/ranged) <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 10%/8% (melee/ranged)</li>
<li>Attack Speed per Stack for Melee Users: 10-15% <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 13-18%</li>
<li>Attack Speed per Stack for Ranged Users: 5-9% <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 8-12%</li>
</ul><strong>Tank It or Leave It</strong>
<ul>
<li>Damage Reduction: 30% <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 25%</li>
</ul><strong>The Brutalizer</strong>
<ul>
<li>Lethality: 15 <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 10</li>
</ul><strong>Tormentor</strong>
<ul>
<li>Total Burn Percent Maximum Health Damage: 5% <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 4%</li>
</ul><strong>Trueshot Prodigy</strong>
<ul>
<li>Damage: 200-700 (based on level) (+100% bonus AD) (+90% AP) <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 250-750 (+140% bonus AD) (+100% AP)</li>
</ul><strong>Willing Sacrifice</strong>
<ul>
<li>Current Converted to Shield: 30% <span class="change-indicator">⇒</span> 25%</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">New Arena Challenges</h4>
<ul>
<li>Cream of the Crop: Deal the most damage to champions in the game</li>
<li>Dancing Shoes: Dodge 5 skillshots (ranged untargeted abilities) within 8 seconds</li>
<li>Double Down: Get double kills</li>
<li>The Wall: Take 10,000 pre-mitigation damage from champions in a single fight without dying</li>
<li>Outplaying the Odds: Get kills while more enemy champions than friendly ones are nearby</li>
<li>I've Got You!: Save an ally who would have otherwise taken lethal damage with a heal or shield</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

<header class="header-primary">
<h2 id="patch-bugfixes-and-qol-changes">Bugfixes &amp; QoL Changes</h2>
</header>
<div class="content-border">
<div class="white-stone accent-before">
<div>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Bugfixes</h4>
<ul>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Elise's Q - Venomous Bite's on-hit sound effects to not play correctly while Elise is in Spider Form.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Draven's R to execute himself if it was used in very close proximity to an enemy and the amount of gold accumulated from his passive was greater than his current health.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Xayah's empowered auto attack feathers to break when hitting a dashing target.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Morgana's W - Tormented Shadow pool VFX to not appear to enemies if it was cast inside of terrain.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Evelynn's Q sound effects to not play when used very close to the target,</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Neeko to be able to inherit the attributes of 2 different units at the same time, causing her to sometimes have 2.5 Attack Speed.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused some of Ornn's upgraded Mythic Items to not grant stackable unique passives such as Rod of Ages or Guinsoos.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that caused Viego to be unable to swap guns if he possessed Aphelios.</li>
</ul>
<hr class="divider"/>
<h4 class="change-detail-title">Cosmetic Bugfixes</h4>
<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue where Hextech Annie's Fire VFX in her idle animation would disappear momentarily.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where Ashen Slayer Sylas, Battle Wolf Sylas, Prestige PROJECT: Sylas and Project Sylas' clone model had corrupted textures when stealing Shaco's Ultimate from the following Shaco skins: Prestige Soul Fighter, Soul Fighter, Winterblessed, Crime City Nightmare and Arcanist.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where High Noon Senna missed transitions when exiting from Homeguard Run animation.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where VFX of Project Senna's Dawning Shadow (R) was no longer cut off near elevation change, when cast from lower ground</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
